Multichar_Symbols

! Tags for POS
 +N +A +Adv +V
 +Pron +CS +CC +Adp +Po +Pr +Interj +Pcle +Num 
 +Coll ! Collective numerals

! Tags for sub-POS
 +Prop +Pers +Dem +Interr +Refl +Recipr +Rel +Indef

 +Use/Sub   ! substandard, not in normative fst
 +Use/Marg  ! marginal (?)
 +Use/Circ  ! circular paths (old ^C^)
 +Use/CircN ! circular paths for the numerals (old ^N^)
 +Use/Ped   ! remove from pedagogical speller, not yet utilised
 +Use/NG    ! not-generate, for ped generation isme-ped.fst
 +Use/NA    ! not-analyse, for restricting analyses needed for 
            ! MT generation not to pop up elsewhere
 +Dial/-KJ  ! forms not in use in KJ (Kárásjohka)
 +Dial/-GG  ! forms not in use in GG (Guovdageaidnu)
 +Dial/-GS  ! forms not in use in GS (Gárasavvon)
 +Dial/KJ   ! forms only in use in KJ
 +Dial/GG   ! forms only in use in GG
 +Dial/GS   ! forms only in use in GS


! Normative/prescriptive compounding tags
! (to govern compound behaviour for the speller, ie what a compound SHOULD BE):

 +First +Last ! Spellertag: Can be first/last member of compound
 +None        ! Spellertag: Can not participate in compounds
 +CmpOnly     ! spellertag: can *only* participate in compounds
 +SgNomLeft +SgGenLeft +PlGenLeft +SgLeft ! Restriction on compound to the left
 +AllCmp      ! Allow all compounding patterns
 +DefSgGenCmp +DefPlGenCmp +DefCmp ! Default values
! to be renamed:  +§SgNomCmp +§SgGenCmp +§PlGenCmp

 +CmpN/Sg +CmpN/SgN                 ! Can take right compound if self is Sg, SgN 
 +CmpN/SgG +CmpN/PlG                ! Can take right compound if self is SgG, PlG 
 +CmpN/First +CmpN/Last             ! prefix only
 +CmpN/None +CmpN/Only              ! prefix only
 +CmpN/Pref                         ! prefix only
 +CmpN/SgLeft +CmpN/SgNomLeft       ! Can take left compound if self is Sg, SgNom
 +CmpN/SgGenLeft +CmpN/PlGenLeft    ! Can take left compound if self is SgGen, … 
 +CmpN/All                          ! 
 +CmpN/Def +CmpN/DefSgGen +CmpN/DefPlGen

! Tags for compound analysis - this is what a compound is:
 +SgCmp +SgNomCmp +SgGenCmp +PlGenCmp +Cmpnd +LCmpnd+ +Guess +ShCmp !testing ShCmp

! Tags for Case and Number Inflection
 +Sg +Du +Pl                           ! Number
 +Ess +Nom +Gen +Acc +Ill +Loc +Com +Com/Sh    ! Case

! Possessive tags
 +PxSg1 +PxSg2 +PxSg3 +PxDu1 +PxDu2 +PxDu3 +PxPl1 +PxPl2 +PxPl3
 +Comp +Superl
 +Attr +Card
 +Ord 
 +Ind +Prs +Prt +Pot +Cond +Imprt
 +Sg1 +Sg2 +Sg3 +Du1 +Du2 +Du3 +Pl1 +Pl2 +Pl3
 +Inf +Ger +ConNeg +ConNegII +Neg +ImprtII +PrsPrc +PrfPrc +Sup +VGen +VAbess
 +Actio +Actor 
 +ABBR +ACR +CLB +PUNCT +LEFT +RIGHT ^GUESSNOUNROOT
 +TV +IV ! Transitivity tags
 +Multi ! Multiword phrase tag
 +G3 ! Grade 3 for homonymies
 +Guess ! for the name guesser
 +v1 +v2 +v3 +v4 +v5  ! Versions 

 +ComPxCPlCom +PxCPlComRecipr ! used in pronoun-sme-morph.txt

! Tags for derivation:

! Old tags:
! +Der/adda +Der/ahtti +Der/alla +Der/asti +Der/easti +Der/aš +Der/d +Der/eamoš
! +Der/amoš +Der/eapmi +Der/geahtes +Der/gielat !better: +Der/NuA
! +Der/h +Der/heapmi +Der/hudda +Der/huhtti +Der/huvva +Der/halla +Der/j +Der/l
! +Der/laš +Der/las +Der/hat +Der/meahttun +Der/muš +Der/n +Der/š +Der/st
! +Der/stuvva +Der/upmi +Der/supmi +Der/vuohta +Der/goahti
! +Der/lágan +Der/lágán +Der/lágaš +Der/jagáš
! +Dimin +Der/viđá +Der/viđi +Der/veara

! Old tags remaining to be checked for the new +Der123 tags:
!+Der/eaddji  ! XN = +Actor

! Explanation:
! Combinations 1, 2, 3, 12, 23, 13, 123 are ok, all other ones are blocked.
! The suffixes marked as +Der1+Der2 to the right cannot combine with Der2, they
! have already "saturated" their Der2-part.
! Phonotactically, Der1 are initial consonants C, Der2 are VCV, and
! Der2 are of a different kind, more like compounding.
! This whole Der123 business is to prevent back-derivation of
! boahtigoahtijuvvohallat and the like.
! Computationally, this is done as a filter composed on top of sme.save.

! Der#begin
! Derivation position in a derivation row:  Affix and
! 1              2            3            4             POS type
+Der1          +Der2        +Der3		+Der4
! Der#1
+Der/t                                                   ! NN
+Der/ár                                                  !ACRO>N
+Der/Dimin                                               ! NN (was: Der/aš & Der/š)
+Der/laš                                                 ! NA
+Der/meahttun                                            ! VA
+Der/d                                                   ! VV
+Der/h                                                   ! VV - -hit/Causative
+Der/huhtti                                              ! VV
+Der/j                                                   ! VV
+Der/l                                                   ! VV
+Der/st                                                  ! VV
+Der/las                                                 ! VA * +Der1+Der2 - can only combine with Der3
+Der/heapmi                                              ! NA * +Der1+Der2 - can only combine with Der3
+Der/lágan                                               ! AA * +Der1+Der2 - can only combine with Der3
+Der/lágán                                               ! AA * +Der1+Der2 - can only combine with Der3
+Der/halla                                               ! VV * +Der1+Der2 - can only combine with Der3
+Der/huvva                                               ! VV * +Der1+Der2 - can only combine with Der3
+Der/stuvva                                              ! VV * +Der1+Der2 - can only combine with Der3
! Der#2
              +Actor
              +Der/Dimin                                 ! NN
              +Der/eapmi                                 ! VN
              +Der/adda                                  ! VV
              +Der/ahtti                                 ! VV
              +Der/alla                                  ! VV
              +Der/asti                                  ! VV
              +Der/at                                    ! QA ! check this!
              +Der/easti                                 ! VV
              +Der/gielat                                ! QA
              +Der/jagáš                                 ! QA
              +Der/lágaš                                 ! QA
              +Der/lágáš                                 ! QA ! Check this!
              +Der/lágan                                 ! AA ! Check these!
              +Der/lágán                                 ! AA ! Check these!
! Der#3                    
                           +Der/PassL                    ! VV - long passive
                           +Der/vuohta                   ! AN
! Der#4                                                            
                                        +Der/goahti      ! VV
                                        +Der/amoš        ! VN
                                        +Der/eamoš       ! VN
                                        +Der/geahtes     ! VA
                                        +Der/muš         ! VN
                                        +Der/supmi       ! VN
                                        +Der/n           ! VN
                                        +Der/upmi        ! VN

! Der#other
! Other/unclassified derivations, can appear in all positions:
+Der/veara    ! NA#
+Der/viđá     ! NA#
!+Der/viđi    ! NA# outcommented, since we have the noun vih0ti, gen:viđi

+Der/PassS    ! VV - short passive

 b9 e7 e9 d9 g8 g9 h8 h9 i7 j9 k9 m8 m9 n8 n9 o7 o9 p9

! Flag diacritics
 @P.NeedNoun.ON@  @D.NeedNoun.ON@  @C.NeedNoun@ ! (Dis)allowing compounds

! @P.Need3Part.ON@ @D.Need3Part.ON@ @C.Need3Part@ !3Part

 @U.Cap.Obl@  @U.Cap.Opt@			! Allowing downcasing of
        							! derived names: deatnulaš.
        							! Actually, downcasing should be obligatory

@U.NeedsVowRed.OFF@    ! This is used to force hyphenation/non-reduction: samediggi-
@U.NeedsVowRed.ON@   ! This is used to force reduction w/o hyphen: samedigge#xxx
@C.NeedsVowRed@       ! Clearing this feature, so that it doesn't interfere with further compounding









! Basic lexica, pointing to the other lexicon files
! =================================================


LEXICON Root
 +Use/Circ: Prefixes ;				  	! 
 @U.Cap.Obl@ ProperNoun ;   ! These flags are for
 @U.Cap.Opt@ ProperNoun ;   ! downcasing the propernouns
! AspellProp ;			    ! Only for aspell target !!
 NounRoot ;
! AspellAffix ;			    ! Only for aspell target !!
! ProperNounFirstPart ;	  ! Merged with ProperNoun, but kept as group
 Adjective ;
 Verb ;
 Copula ;
 Negativeverb ;
 Adverb ;
 Particles ;
 Subjunction ;
 Conjunction ;
 Adposition ;
 Interjection ;
 Pronoun ;
! +Use/CircN: Numeral ;	  Circular 
 Numeral ;	! we need numerals for Apertium.
 Acronym ;
 Abbreviation ;
 Punctuation ;
 MiddleNouns ; ! gaskbeaivi, this is the "new" R, not Rreal




! Prefixing and compounding
! =========================

LEXICON Prefixes
 ii%-+Use/Circ:ii%- Adjective;        !    ii-biologalaš 
 ii%-+Use/Circ:ii%- Noun;			 
 Lulle%-+Use/Circ:Lul^le%- ProperNoun;        ! Lulli-Trøndelaga etc.
 Lulli%-+Use/Circ:Lul^li%- ProperNoun;       
 Lullinuorta%-+Use/Circ:Lul^li^nuor^ta%- ProperNoun;
 Mátta%-+Use/Circ:Mát^ta%- ProperNoun;       
 Davvi%-+Use/Circ:Dav^vi%- ProperNoun;       
 Davve%-+Use/Circ:Dav^ve%- ProperNoun;        ! 76 i korpus, 17 i leksikon
 Gaska%-+Use/Circ:Gas^ka%- ProperNoun;      
 Vuolli%-+Use/Circ:Vuol^li%- ProperNoun;      
 Vuolle%-+Use/Circ:Vuol^le%- ProperNoun;      
 Badje%-+Use/Circ:Bad^je%- ProperNoun;       
 Oarje%-+Use/Circ:Oar^je%- ProperNoun;       
 Orjjel%-+Use/Circ:Orj^jel%- ProperNoun;      ! Orjje 0 i korpus  orjjelsápmi
 Orjješ%-+Use/Circ:Orj^ješ%- ProperNoun;     
 Mátta%-+Use/Circ:Mát^ta%- ProperNoun;       
 Nuorta%-+Use/Circ:Nuor^ta%- ProperNoun;     
 Ođđa%-+Use/Circ:Ođ^đa%- ProperNoun;        
 eahpe#+Use/Circ:eah^pe# Noun;          
 eahpe#+Use/Circ:eah^pe# Adjective;     
 eahpe#+Use/Circ:eah^pe# Verb;          

!"<Jus fylkkaboazodoallostivra gávnnaha ahte>"
!"<Ođđa siidaoasi dohkkeheami biehttaleami>"

LEXICON R    ! lexicalising the 3-part compounds, with the tag ShCmp
    Rreal ;  ! Business as usual: Normal compounds right on to Rreal
 #  MiddleNouns ; ! These nouns should not return to themselves, to avoid -jotjotjot-
                  ! They thus point directly to Rreal.
 
LEXICON Rreal ! This is the former R lexicon, renamed to avoid the MiddleNouns loop
                #@U.NeedsVowRed.ON@@C.NeedsVowRed@+Use/Circ:#@U.NeedsVowRed.ON@@C.NeedsVowRed@ Noun ;                     ! This is the normal case.		         
 #@P.NeedNoun.ON@@U.NeedsVowRed.ON@@C.NeedsVowRed@+Use/Circ:#@P.NeedNoun.ON@@U.NeedsVowRed.ON@@C.NeedsVowRed@ Verb ;      ! Flag diacr declares that the compound   
 #@P.NeedNoun.ON@@U.NeedsVowRed.ON@@C.NeedsVowRed@+Use/Circ:#@P.NeedNoun.ON@@U.NeedsVowRed.ON@@C.NeedsVowRed@ Adjective ; ! needs a N tag later in the derivation  
           +Hyph#@U.NeedsVowRed.ON@@C.NeedsVowRed@+Use/Circ:%-@U.NeedsVowRed.ON@@C.NeedsVowRed@ Noun ;                    ! These 3 cases add a hyphen, so     
 +Hyph#@P.NeedNoun.ON@@U.NeedsVowRed.ON@@C.NeedsVowRed@+Use/Circ:%-@P.NeedNoun.ON@@U.NeedsVowRed.ON@@C.NeedsVowRed@  Verb ;      ! Sem-julggaštus and maana-gåetie	      
 +Hyph#@P.NeedNoun.ON@@U.NeedsVowRed.ON@@C.NeedsVowRed@+Use/Circ:%-@P.NeedNoun.ON@@U.NeedsVowRed.ON@@C.NeedsVowRed@  Adjective ; ! are allowed.			              

 %-#@U.NeedsVowRed.OFF@@C.NeedsVowRed@+Use/Circ:%-#@U.NeedsVowRed.OFF@@C.NeedsVowRed@ Acronym ;    ! maana-tv, "lomme-cd-spelar"
 %-#@U.NeedsVowRed.OFF@@C.NeedsVowRed@+Use/Circ:%-#@U.NeedsVowRed.OFF@@C.NeedsVowRed@ ProperNoun ; ! Proper nouns as the 2nd part of compounds for non-hyph.
                               ! words. viessu-London goes through here.

 %-#@U.NeedsVowRed.ON@@C.NeedsVowRed@+Use/Circ:%-#@U.NeedsVowRed.ON@@C.NeedsVowRed@ HyphNouns ; ! Go to words requiring hyphens, like -tv- and -cd-

 @U.NeedsVowRed.ON@@C.NeedsVowRed@+Cmpnd:%@U.NeedsVowRed.ON@@C.NeedsVowRed@- ENDLEX ;     ! This to take care of Oahpo- ja dutkandept - want this in speller
 R-LAGAN ;


LEXICON RHyph ! Recursive lexicon from all classes REQUIRING a hyphen to follow.
              ! NBNBNB!!! The hyphen should be added here! NOT in the other lexicons!

 %-#+Use/Circ:%-# Noun;                                     ! This is the normal case.
 %-#@P.NeedNoun.ON@+Use/Circ:%-#@P.NeedNoun.ON@ Verb;       ! Flag diacr declares that the compound
 %-#@P.NeedNoun.ON@+Use/Circ:%-#@P.NeedNoun.ON@ Adjective ; ! needs a N tag later in the derivation

 %-#+Use/Circ:%-# Acronym ;    ! maana-tv, "lomme-cd-spelar"
 %-#+Use/Circ:%-# ProperNoun ; ! Proper nouns as the 2nd part of compounds for hyph-words.
                               ! London-Hull is covered here, whereas Hull-viessu
                               ! is covered by RHyph + Noun.

 %-#+Use/Circ:%-# HyphNouns ; ! Go to words requiring hyphens, like -tv- and -cd-

 +Cmpnd:%- ENDLEX ;      ! This to take care of Oahpo- ja dutkandept - want this in speller

! Proper noun compounds without hyphens are NOT presently covered - if they were
! to be added, they need to be marked +Use/Sub. Examples: LondonHull & viessuLondon.


LEXICON Rnoun
 Rreal ;                   ! Going to the compound lexicon
 +N+Attr+Use/Sub: ENDLEX ; ! Kárášjot, as independent (sub) word

LEXICON R-LAGAN
 +Der1+Der/lágan+Use/Circ:»lágan LAGAN ; ! ! biilalágan, 
   ! noaidelágán noaiddilágán beatnagalágán beanalágán all these goes
  ! Nielsen:beatnatlágán, beatnatlágáš, beanalágáš, giđalágáš, áhččelágáš,
 +Der1+Der/lágán+Use/Circ:»lágán LAGAN ; ! ! Oslolágán
 +Der1+Der/lágaš+Use/Circ:»lágaž LAGAN ; ! ! etc.
 +Der1+Der/lágáš+Use/Circ:»lágáž LAGAN ;

LEXICON GOAHTI !Bisyll. V-Nouns. Short nom-compound-forms goahte-,long/short gen
 +N:%> GOAHTICMP ;
 +N+Sg+Nom:%> K ;
 +N+Sg+Nom+Use/Ped:%> Px3V ;
 +N+Der/viđá+Adv:»X7viđá K ;
! +N+Der/viđi+Adv:»X7viđi K ;
 +N:%> EssV ;
 +N:%> GOAHTI-OBL ;
 +N: DenominalAdjsV1 ;
 +N: DenominalAdjsV2 ;
 +N: DenominalNounsV ;

LEXICON GOAHTI-IU !Bisyll. V-Nouns. Short nom-compound-forms goahte-,long/short gen
 +N:%> GOAHTICMP ;
 +N+Sg+Nom:%> K ;
 +N+Sg+Nom+Use/Ped:%> Px3V ;
 +N+Der/viđá+Adv:»X7viđá K ;
! +N+Der/viđi+Adv:»X7viđi K ;
 +N:%> EssV ;
 +N:%> GOAHTI-IU-OBL ;
 +N: DenominalAdjsV1 ;
 +N: DenominalAdjsV2 ;
 +N: DenominalNounsV ;


LEXICON GOAHTILONG !Long nom-compound-forms,long gen
 +N:%> GOAHTILONGCMP ;
 +N+Sg+Nom:%> K ;
 +N+Sg+Nom+Use/Ped:%> Px3V ;
 +N+Der/viđá+Adv:»viđá K ;
! +N+Der/viđi+Adv:»viđi K ;
 +N:%> EssV ;
 +N:%>X2 GOAHTA- ; ! Px sublexicon
 +N:%>X3 GOAHTAI ; ! Ill sublexicon
 +N+Use/Sub:%> GOAHTAI ; ! Ill sublexicon
 +N:%>X4 GOADI- ; ! weak grade abs decl
 +N:%>%^DISIMP GODII- ; ! weak gr dipth simpl
 +N+Use/Sub:%>X5 GODII- ; ! weak gr dipth simpl
 +N:%>X6 GOADA- ; ! AG Px
 +N: DenominalAdjsV1 ;
 +N: DenominalAdjsV2 ;
 +N: DenominalNounsV ;

LEXICON GOAHTILONGSHORT !Sometimes long nom-compound-forms,long gen
 +N:%> GOAHTILONGSHORTCMP ;
 +N+Sg+Nom:%> K ;
 +N+Sg+Nom+Use/Ped:%> Px3V ;
 +N+Der/viđá+Adv:»X7viđá K ;
! +N+Der/viđi+Adv:»X7viđi K ;
 +N:%> EssV ;
 +N:%>X2 GOAHTA- ; ! Px sublexicon
 +N:%>X3 GOAHTAI ; ! Ill sublexicon
 +N+Use/Sub:%> GOAHTAI ; ! Ill sublexicon
 +N:%>X4 GOADI- ; ! weak grade abs decl
 +N+Use/Sub:%>X5 GODII- ; ! weak gr dipth simpl
 +N:%>%^DISIMP GODII- ; ! weak gr dipth simpl
 +N:%>X6 GOADA- ; ! AG Px
! +N:%>X8 GOADE- ; ! Ditto (?)
! +N+SgGenCmp:%>X8 R ;
 +N: DenominalAdjsV1 ;
 +N: DenominalAdjsV2 ;
 +N: DenominalNounsV ;

LEXICON ALBMI !Bisyll. V-Nouns. Short nom-compound-forms, long gen.
 +N:%> GOAHTICMP ;
 +N+Sg+Nom:%> K ;
 +N+Sg+Nom+Use/Ped:%> Px3V ;
 +N+Der/viđá+Adv:»X7viđá K ;
 +N:%> EssV ;
 +N:%>X2 GOAHTA- ; ! Px sublexicon

 +A:%>X7 NomVadj "good A" ;
 +A:%>X1 EssVadj "good A" ;
 +A:%>X7 EssVadj ;
 +A:%>   GOAHTI-OBLadj "good A" ;

! Comparative and superlative
 +A+Comp:%>X8b BUStem ;
 +A+Superl:%>X8muss BUOREMUS ;

! +A+Der1+Der2+Der/lágan:»X4lágan LAGAN ;
! +A+Der1+Der2+Der/lágan:»X7lágan LAGAN ;

 +A#+Use/Circ:»X7# ALIT ;  ! both comp and independent adj. Here for ditto reason.

 : K ;                  ! Plain attributive

 #+Use/Circ:»# ALIT ; ! both comp and independent adj !

 +Use/Sub: Rreal ;

 #+Use/Sub+Use/Circ:»# ALIT ;  ! both comp and independent adj

 +Imprt+Use/Sub:eah'ki%> ImprtVB ;
 +Imprt+Dial/%-KJ:eatni%> ImprtV2 ;
 +Imprt+Sg1:ehko%>n ENDLEX ;
 +Imprt+Sg3:ehko%>s ENDLEX ;
 +Imprt+Sg3+Use/NG:us ENDLEX ;     
 +Imprt+Du2:eahkki%> ENDLEX ;
 +Imprt+Du3:ehko%>ska ENDLEX ;
 +Imprt+Pl1+Dial/%-GG:ehko%>t ENDLEX ;	! 
 +Imprt+Pl1+Dial/%-KJ:eatno%>t ENDLEX ;   ! 
 +Imprt+Pl2:ehke%>t ENDLEX ;
 +Imprt+Pl3:ehko%>set ENDLEX ;
